DETECTOR   (SCIN) Neutrons and gamma rays were detected using     14726  1   13 
           array of 54 EJ-309 liquid scintillator detectors each  14726  1   14 
           with an R4144 Hamamatsu PMT readout. Detectors are     14726  1   15 
           placed at nine evenly spaced polar angles from         14726  1   16 
           30 deg to 150 deg with respect to the beam direction,  14726  1   17 
           and at azimuthal angles of +-24 deg, 57 deg  and       14726  1   18

METHOD     (TOF,PSD,COINC) The measurements were carried out at   14726  1   20 
           WNR flight path 15L, located 21.5 m from the spallation14726  1   21 
           target and 15 deg to the left of the incident pulsed   14726  1   22 
           proton beam axis. Each proton micropulse was a 150-ps  14726  1   23 
           wide, separated by approximately 1.8 mu-s from         14726  1   24 
           neighboring micropulse. Each macropulse consists of    14726  1   25 
           approximately 347 micropulses. WNR received an average 14726  1   26 
           of 100 macropulses per second during this experiment.  14726  1   27 
           A timing signal, was provided to the experimental area 14726  1   28 
           indicating each new proton micropulse. Signals from    14726  1   29 
           detectors were digitized. Neutron and gamma signals    14726  1   30 
           were separated based on the PSD ratio of the pulse     14726  1   31 
           tail integral to the full pulse integral.              14726  1   32 
           Coincidences were assembled offline                    14726  1   33 
CORRECTION Corrections for in target multiple scattering          14726  1   34 
           were applied                                           14726  1   35
